submitqc is the Tiny Core extension submission quality testing tool.
This unstable release (20241219) is UNDER TESTING for TC5+, x86/x86_64/armv7.
In particular, feedback/testing on Pi/ARM usage is welcome!

Usage: submitqc [-?|-h|--help] [--kernel=KVER] [--nonet] [--no-fix]
   [--tcz=TCZFILE] [TCZFILE] [--changes] [--license] [--no-load]
   [--blocksize=BLOCKSIZE]

Run submitqc in the same directory as your extension(s). It will find &
   test tcz files in the run directory.

Options:

  -c --color		Use colored text output
  --kernel=KVER		Test modules using KVER (default: `uname -r`)
  --core=TCVER		Refer to online repo for core TCVER (default: `version`)
  --arch=ARCH		Refer to online repo for architecture ARCH (default: `uname -m`)
  --libs		Try dynamic library inclusion tests (unstable; time-consuming)
  --nonet		Disable network-based checks
  --no-fix		Don't fix chmod/chown inconsistencies (default: fix)
  --strip		Strip any unstripped binaries (default: warn)
  --changes		View change and planning details
  --self-package	Self-package under /tmp/submitqc-pkg/
  --license		View license details (GNU GPLv2)
  --no-load		Don't load any required extensions (coreutils, squashfs-tools, etc.)
  --blocksize=BLOCKSIZE	Blocksize in Bytes (default: 4096) (only for 64-bit)

submitqc is distributed under the terms of the GNU GPLv2. see --license.
